REFERENCES documents(id) ON DELETE SET NULL` — deleting a document now nulls the link instead of dangling it. All write/read paths updated to pass/compare `UUID` objects: `fhir_service.create_observation` (validates the UUID, drops malformed), `ai.pipeline.persistence` (`find_source_doc` returns the UUID; `save_observation` typed `Optional[UUID]`), `analytics_service` (removed the `cast(id, String)` and `str()`-compare smell — now plain `UUID == UUID`), `document_service_db` (UUID lookup + `::uuid`-cast raw SQL). Schema field `Optional[UUID]`. 3 regression tests (`test_audit_b2_document_id_fk.py`) prove the column type, FK rejection of a non-existent document, and the on-delete SET NULL cascade.

- **Data architecture (audit B1): per-tenant uniqueness for catalog/identity columns.** `slug`/`mrn` were `UNIQUE` globally on four tables even though `tenant_id` is nullable — so a system-wide (NULL tenant) row and a tenant override could not share a slug, and two tenants could not each carry a patient with the same MRN. Replaced the global unique with a `(col, COALESCE(tenant_id, <sentinel>))` unique index (the pattern already proven on `concepts`, migration `9a3f7c2e1b4d`) on `biomarker_definitions.slug`, `anatomy_structures.slug`, `clinical_event_types.slug`, and `fhir_patients.mrn` (migration `l3c4d5e6f7a8`). NULL-tenant (system) rows collapse into one synthetic tenant so two system rows still collide, while a system row and a tenant row — or two tenant rows — no longer do. **Deliberately excluded:** `users.email` (remains globally unique — it is the login identifier and `get_user_by_email` uses `scalar_one_or_none()`; the model is one-tenant-per-user) and `units.symbol` (no `tenant_id` column — units are a universal reference catalog). The global unique was strictly stricter than per-tenant, so the upgrade cannot fail on a populated DB. 3 regression tests (`test_audit_b1_tenant_unique.py`).

- **Data integrity (audit B10): added the obvious CHECK constraints.** The schema had exactly one `CHECK` (Patient `mrn_not_empty`); the rest of the domain invariants were enforced only by convention / application code, so a bad seed or a stray write silently stored unusable rows. Added 8 constraints (declared on the models' `__table_args__` + migration `k2b3c4d5e6f7`): `units.conversion_multiplier > 0`; `biomarker_definitions.reference_range_min <= reference_range_max` (NULLs allowed — an inverted range yields a nonsensical `relative_score`); `examinations.extraction_progress` / `documents.progress` / `export_jobs.progress` / `import_jobs.progress` all in `[0, 100]`; `ai_models.max_tokens > 0` and `ai_models.temperature BETWEEN 0 AND 2`. The migration clamps any pre-existing rows that would violate the new constraints before adding them (defensive — the project has no users, but a dev DB may carry seed data). 4 regression tests (`test_audit_b10_check_constraints.py`) assert the models declare the constraints, the DB has them, and enforcement rejects bad rows while accepting good ones.

- **Security (audit D1, frontend): logout no longer leaves cached PHI in IndexedDB.** The logout wipe in `utils/auth.ts` deleted an IndexedDB named `health_assistant-offline` (underscore) while the Dexie store in `services/db.ts` opens `health-assistant-offline` (hyphen), so the offline cache (cached patient data, biomarker trends, the pending-sync queue) survived across user switches on any browser where the `indexedDB.databases()` bulk-delete fallback is unavailable (Firefox/Safari — Chromium-only API). The DB name is now a single exported constant (`OFFLINE_DB_NAME`) in `db.ts`, imported by the logout wipe, so the two can never drift again. New `performTenantSwitch` regression test (below).
- **Fix (audit D5, frontend): `performTenantSwitch` no longer fires the token callback twice.** A duplicated `onTokensUpdated(...)` call (+ duplicate comment) meant the token setter ran twice on every tenant switch — harmless today but a real latent defect (any side-effect in the callback would double-apply). Removed the duplicate; new `performTenantSwitch.test.ts` pins that the callback fires exactly once.

- **Cleanup (audit E1–E6): deleted 5 dead files + retired the stub-`User` test mock.** Removed `app/models/tenant.py`, `app/models/document.py` (zero-reference non-SQLAlchemy stub classes whose real models are `*_model.py`), the merge artifacts `app/models/enums.py.orig` / `enums.py.patch`, and the placeholder `app/services/base.py`. The `app/models/user.py` stub `User` was only ever a 4-field mock shell used by `test_auth.py`/`test_users.py`; both now construct a transient real `UserModel` (with proper `Role` enum + `UUID` `tenant_id`) so they exercise the actual model instead of validating nothing. Zero behaviour change; 1805-test collection and the two affected suites are green.

- **Security (audit A1, critical): closed a second-order SQL-injection in the telemetry analytics path.** The biomarker `slug` is f-string-interpolated into raw SQL in `analytics_service.get_biomarker_trends` (`CAST(data->>'{slug}' AS FLOAT)` / `data ? '{slug}'`). Because `slug` is a user-writable string (any authenticated `USER` can `POST /biomarkers/` with `is_telemetry=true`), a crafted slug could exfiltrate cross-tenant data via UNION/error channels. Fixed with three layers of defence: (1) the `BiomarkerCreate` Pydantic schema now validates `slug` against `^[A-Za-z0-9_-]{1,80}$` on the API write path (input-only — the response schema still serialises any pre-existing row); (2) `analytics_service` now refuses to interpolate any slug that is not a strict identifier — unsafe slugs are skipped with a warning rather than interpolated (defence-in-depth, catches pre-existing rows or AI-pipeline/import writes that bypass the schema); (3) the AI ontology pipeline sanitises its AI-proposed slugs (`sanitize_slug`) before any DB lookup/insert so auto-expanded catalog entries are always safe. New helpers `is_safe_slug` / `sanitize_slug` in `schemas/biomarker.py`. 26 new regression tests (`test_audit_a1_slug_injection.py`) including an end-to-end test asserting an injection-payload slug never reaches the executed SQL.

- **Security (audit A6): endpoints no longer leak internal exception detail via `detail=str(e)`.** Broad `except Exception` blocks in the documents, import, AI-assistance, biomarker, and admin endpoints forwarded raw exception messages to clients (DB constraint names, file paths, PHI). Now 500-class errors re-raise so the global handler returns a generic 500 + correlation id; 400-class errors log server-side and return a generic message. Document upload no longer echoes the caller's `tenant_id` in the "Tenant not found" message. 10 regression tests (`test_audit_a6_error_leak.py`) statically assert the previously-leaky endpoints never embed `str(e)` in client detail.

- **Security (audit A3 + A4): upload file-type validation + inline-download XSS hardening + upload-size enforcement.** The document upload path accepted any file type and served downloads `inline` with no `nosniff`, so an uploaded `.svg`/`.html` ran as stored XSS at the app origin; `MAX_UPLOAD_SIZE` (50 MB) was defined but never checked, so a single request could exhaust server RAM. Fixed: (1) uploads are now restricted to a medical-document allowlist (PDF/images/DICOM/text — deliberately excluding `svg`/`html`/`xml`/`js` active-content types); (2) the download endpoint forces `Content-Disposition: attachment` for active-content extensions and sets `X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff` on every served file (defence-in-depth even if a bad type slipped past the allowlist); (3) uploads are read in 1 MiB chunks and rejected with `413` if they exceed the cap (`_read_capped`). 39 regression tests (`test_audit_a3_a4_upload_security.py`).

- **Security (audit A7–A13): medium/low hardening batch.** (A7) Every response now carries baseline security headers (`X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff`, `X-Frame-Options: DENY`, `Referrer-Policy`, `Strict-Transport-Security`). (A8) The prompt-injection guard gains an env-gated block mode — `PROMPT_GUARD_BLOCK_HIGH=true` forces high-risk inputs to be flagged for rejection at the boundary (off by default; HITL remains the structural defence). (A9) Removed the `print("[WS-DEBUG]…")` statements that leaked token-existence and user IDs to stdout. (A10) `get_document()` now takes an optional `tenant_id` and scopes the query; the authenticated document CRUD endpoints pass it (SYSTEM_ADMIN bypasses) so a forgotten re-check can't read cross-tenant. (A11) `encrypt_secret` fails closed (`RuntimeError`) in non-dev environments when `INTEGRATION_SECRET_KEY` is unset instead of silently storing plaintext; dev/test keeps the loud-warning fallback. (A12) The deprecated `?token=` WebSocket fallback now emits a deprecation warning. (A13) The anatomy-figure slug is sanitised to a strict basename with a containment check (`relative_to`) before any file write, blocking path traversal. 11 regression tests (`test_audit_a7_a13_hardening.py`).

- **Security (audit A2): Redis-backed rate limiting on authentication endpoints.** `/auth/login` (20/min), `/auth/register` (5/min), `/auth/refresh` (30/min), and `/auth/invite` (10/min) are now rate-limited per client IP via fixed-window Redis counters (`app/core/rate_limit.py`) so the limit holds across all workers. Degrades open (allows requests) if Redis is unreachable — rate limiting is defence-in-depth, not an availability gate. 7 regression tests (`test_audit_a2_rate_limit.py`).

- **Security (audit A5): refresh-token rotation + revocation.** Refresh tokens now carry a `type=refresh` claim and a unique `jti` tracked server-side in Redis (`app/core/token_store.py`). `/auth/refresh` **rotates**: the consumed `jti` is revoked and a brand-new refresh token is issued on every call (previously the same long-lived token was returned indefinitely, so a stolen token granted access for its full lifetime with no server-side invalidation). New `POST /auth/logout` (revoke one refresh token) and `POST /auth/logout-all` (revoke every refresh token for the user). An access token can no longer be replayed at `/auth/refresh` (the `type` claim is enforced). Degrades open if Redis is down. 9 regression tests (`test_audit_a5_refresh_rotation.py`). **Breaking:** clients must now use the *new* refresh token returned by each `/auth/refresh` call (rotation); old refresh tokens are single-use.

- **Fix: idempotent re-seed no longer nullifies `anatomy_structures.class_concept_id`.** The seed update path overwrote `class_concept_id` unconditionally — when `resolve_concept_by_slug` returned `None` (e.g. a concept missing its `ANATOMY_CLASS` kind tag from a prior partial seed), a valid class link was destroyed. The update path now only overwrites when resolution succeeds, preserving existing data. The `test_seed_order` regression test is reset-deterministic (wipes `anatomy_structures` first) so it no longer depends on accumulated test-DB state.

- **Test suite: all 18 pre-existing failures fixed (suite now fully green — 1738 passed).** Stale mock in `test_ocr_persistence_scoring` updated to include `class_concept`; obsolete `test_examination_categories_endpoints` removed (the router was deleted in the taxonomy unification — the RBAC property it guarded is now covered by `test_catalog_rbac`); `test_catalog_exact_match` updated to assert the hybrid (trigram+FTS+RRF) search that intentionally replaced the old substring-ILIKE; `test_audit_a1` slug-rejection cases moved to `BiomarkerCreate` (input-only validation).

- **Sidebar nav restructured: Patient Record/Clinical Data merged, Catalogs flattened, Notifications promoted.** The main sidebar had a conceptually muddy boundary — "Patient Record" (9 items) and "Clinical Data" (2 items) overlapped (biomarkers/medications are clinical data; examinations/documents are patient record), and "Patient Record" was an unstructured grab-bag mixing identity, analytics, treatments, alerts, and time-views. Changes: (1) **Clinical Data is merged into Patient Record**, now organised with internal `section` dividers (the same mechanism the Administration group already used) — *Clinical Record* (Examinations, Documents, Biomarkers, Correlative Analytics), *Treatments & Alerts* (Medications, Vaccinations, Allergy Alerts), *Timeline* (Clinical Events, Clinical Calendar) — so the 10-item group is scannable instead of a flat list. (2) **Notifications promoted to a top-level item** — it is app-level (a header bell already exists), not patient-scoped, so it no longer sits under Patient Record. (3) **Catalogs collapsed from a 6-item expanding group to a single flat link** — `/catalogs` already opens a unified tabbed workspace; the six `?type=` sub-items were redundant shortcuts that added nav noise. Result: 5 top-level items (Dashboard, Patient Record, Notifications, Catalogs, AI Assistant) + role-gated Administration, down from 6, with the mega-group made navigable via sections. New i18n keys (`section_clinical_record`/`section_treatments_alerts`/`section_timeline`) added to en + el; `clinical_data` key retained for compatibility.

- **Catalog: unified filter UI (all dropdown FacetChips) + category tag on every row + selected-value pills.** Filters were applied inconsistently across catalog types — `concept` (kind) and `anatomy` (class) used inline toggle chips in the toolbar while `biomarker`/`allergy`/`vaccine`/`medication` used popover-dropdown `FacetChip`s in a second toolbar row. Both are now **server-side `FacetChip` dropdowns** (`conceptKindFacet` with static `ConceptKind` enum options; `anatomy` class facet with fetched `anatomy_class` options via a `makeClassFacet` factory in `catalogFacetRegistry`), so every catalog type uses the same dropdown component and filtering composes correctly with pagination (server-side, before `limit`/`offset`) rather than only over the loaded 50-item page. The previously-dead `catalogFilter.serverParams` (computed by `useFilterState` but never consumed) is now wired into the `load()`/`loadMore()` API calls, with a stringified `serverFilterKey` dependency so client-side facet toggles don't trigger a refetch. Row tags were equally uneven — only `biomarker` and `anatomy` surfaced their category as a colored `ClassBadge`; `medication`/`allergy`/`vaccine`/`concept` showed only the scope badge. The three FHIR-catalog `to_dict()` methods now emit `class_concept_slug` + `class_concept_name` (the `class_concept` relationship is already `lazy="selectin"`, so no N+1) and concepts now surface `primary_kind` as a colored `KIND_COLORS` badge (concepts carry no class FK). The generic `ClassBadge` in `CatalogBrowser` falls back to `primary_kind` when no `class_concept` is present, and its click-to-filter now routes to the matching facet (kind for concepts, class otherwise). Finally, the removable **active-value pills** built into `FacetChip` (`showActivePills`) are now enabled in both the catalog workspace and the picker browse modal, so selected filter values render as removable chips next to each dropdown without having to open it (desktop-only; mobile sees the count summary on the trigger). Tests updated (facet registry + facet defs); `CatalogToolbar` lost the inline-chip props/render. The picker modal filters out server-mode facets (kind/class) since it filters in-memory and doesn't refetch.

- **ScaleSlider + occurrence-panel form polish.** (1) New reusable **`ScaleSlider`** (`components/ui/ScaleSlider.tsx`): a bounded number renders as a green→yellow→red gradient slider with a synced numeric input (bidirectionally in sync, clamps to `[min,max]` on blur), a colour-shifting thumb/input border (green=low → red=high via hue interpolation), and optional Mild/Severe captions. Pseudo-element thumb/track CSS lives in `index.css` via a `--scale-thumb-color` custom property. `DynamicMetadataForm` now upgrades any `number` field that declares both `min`+`max` to a `ScaleSlider` automatically (unbounded numbers stay plain inputs; no schema change — the seed's `intensity` already declares `min:1,max:10`). (2) **`MetadataField` gains an optional `placeholder`** (backend Pydantic + frontend type); the pain-episode `trigger` field now carries `"e.g. stress, weather change, lack of sleep"` so users understand its scope. (3) **Episode & Symptom Tracking panel reworked**: the bare `<input type="time">` is replaced with the existing clock-face `TimePicker`; the cramped `AnatomySearchPopup` is replaced with `CatalogField` (`allowedTypes={['anatomy']}`, single-select) matching the Specialized Details body-location picker; the occurrence `location` now stores the `{type,id,label}` selection object; the intensity slider gains the numeric input; and the card is restacked into full-width rows (date/time, intensity, body location) so the body-location field is no longer cropped. `ClinicalEventDetail` renders the occurrence location via `formatMetadataValue` and the now-dead `getBodyPartName`/`bodyParts`/`listBodyParts` cluster is removed. New test pins the `placeholder` round-trip.

- **Catalog picker: graph view + explorer-parity filters (list and graph).** The catalog picker browse modal now has a **List | Graph** toggle, and each view exposes the same filters its catalog-explorer counterpart does. **Graph view** (new `CatalogPickerGraph`, self-contained): renders the ontology graph via `ConceptGraphView` with its own filter strip — multi-select catalog-type chips (color-filled, with live node counts; default to the field's `allowedTypes`, toggle others on for cross-catalog context), multi-select concept-kind chips (hidden when the field locks a `concept_kind`), include-isolated toggle, depth buttons (∞/1–4 BFS from the clicked node), and relation-type chips (reusing `GraphRelationFilter`). Nodes whose catalog type is outside `allowedTypes` render **dimmed + non-clickable** (visible for relational context, never selectable — e.g. for a body-location field you see the full anatomy hierarchy plus connected body systems, but only anatomy nodes are clickable); already-picked nodes get a green accent. **List view**: keeps the type dropdown + scope + search and adds the per-type **`FilterBar`** facets (biomarker category/telemetry/coding/unit, allergy category/is_custom, vaccine coding_system, medication is_custom, concept status) via `useFilterState` + `getFacetsForType`, mirroring the workspace toolbar. `ConceptGraphView` (the shared graph renderer) gains two opt-in props — `disabledNodeIds?: Set<string>` (dim + click-guard) and `pickedNodeIds?: Set<string>` (green accent) — both no-ops when omitted, so the workspace ontology graph and relations graph are unaffected. The graph endpoint caps at 2500 edges with an amber truncation warning; an empty state points to list view when a catalog has no relationships.

- **Typed `metadata_schema` for clinical event types + unified catalog picker in dynamic forms.** `ClinicalEventType.metadata_schema` is now validated by a typed Pydantic model (`MetadataSchema`/`MetadataField`) backed by three new enums (`MetadataFieldType`, `CatalogType`, `CatalogRelationType`) — a malformed seed or API payload raises a precise error instead of silently rendering nothing (fail-loud). The legacy ad-hoc `source: "body-parts"` string is removed (breaking change, no users to migrate); a field now declaratively references any catalog via `{"type": "catalog-select", "catalogs": ["anatomy"]}` and can be narrowed to a concept kind via `concept_kind`. `DynamicMetadataForm` is rewritten with an **exhaustive `switch` over `MetadataFieldType`** (a missing branch is now a TS compile error via a `default: never` guard, closing the dead-`select`/`code`/`options`-rendered-nothing bug class). `catalog-select` fields render through a new thin **`CatalogField`** form wrapper over the existing **`CatalogItemPicker`**, so a metadata field can search any combination of biomarker/medication/allergy/anatomy/vaccine/concept catalogs from the same reusable component; the bespoke **`DynamicAnatomyField` is deleted**. The picked value is stored as `{type, id, label}` (single) or an array (multi); `ClinicalEventDetail` gains a robust `formatMetadataValue` that renders these without `[object Object]`. **`search_catalogs(kind=…)` + `GET /catalogs/search?kind=…`** narrow the concept catalog by `ConceptKind` (unknown kind → 400), letting the same picker power examination/event-category and specialty selection from one endpoint; `CatalogItemPicker` gains a `conceptKind` prop threaded to both inline type-ahead and the browse modal. The browse modal's "All catalogs" option is **disabled when the picker is scoped to a single distinctive catalog** (e.g. body location → anatomy) and now correctly respects `allowedTypes` in "All" mode (was leaking cross-catalog results). A latent infinite-render loop in `CatalogItemPicker` (`allowedTypes?.map(String)` created a new array each render, thrashing `useEffect`) is fixed via `useMemo`. Seed `clinical_event_types.json` migrated to the new shape; `SeedService` validates descriptors on load. 33 new tests (`test_metadata_schema.py`, `test_seed_clinical_event_types.py`, kind-filter cases in `test_catalog_search.py`). Plan: `dev/plans/clinical-event-catalog-fields-2026-07-14.md`.

- **New opencode skill: `documentation`.** A reusable skill (`.opencode/skills/documentation/SKILL.md`) codifying how to create, edit, and position Health Assistant's documentation: the docs architecture (`docs-tree.json` as the single source of truth for public nav + SEO metadata, no YAML frontmatter in markdown), the locked positioning rules (self-hosted, open-source, privacy-first, audience-neutral, FHIR stated but never leading), the SEO keyword priorities, the anti-fluff and anti-overclaim checklist, the internal-vs-public doc boundary, and the step-by-step recipe for adding a new doc. The `project-overview` skill's task→skill table and skill list now reference it.

- **Docs SEO + positioning pass across all public documentation.** Audited all 28 docs for search-engine discoverability (docs are published on the website) and alignment with the self-hosted, open-source, audience-neutral positioning. Changes: (1) **`docs-tree.json` enriched** with a `description` field on all 23 entries — the website consumes these for `<title>`/meta description tags; markdown files stay clean (no YAML frontmatter, which renders as raw text on GitHub). (2) **Six docs with wasted intros rewritten** — ARCHITECTURE, DEVELOPMENT, DEVELOPMENT_PLAN, STATUS, INSTALL, and PROJECT_STRUCTURE previously opened with "See STATUS.md…" (useless as meta descriptions); each now has a real 1–2 sentence description with keywords. (3) **TENANCY_AND_USER_MANAGEMENT.md neutralized** — removed "Home-First, Clinic-Ready" tagline, "Head of Household", "entire family", "family members" as positioning prose; kept `HOUSEHOLD` org-type and "Default Household" where they describe actual code behavior. (4) **Fluffy adjectives toned down** — "comprehensive", "seamlessly", "robust", "powerful", "production-ready" replaced with concrete language across ARCHITECTURE, DEVELOPMENT, STATUS, EXPORT_IMPORT, INTEGRATIONS_SDK, INTEGRATIONS_FRAMEWORK, MOBILE_SYNC_APP, TELEMETRY, SEEDING_AND_DEMOS. (5) **docs-tree.json restructured** — removed 6 internal docs from public navigation (AI_PROVIDER_TESTS, USER_INTEGRATIONS_PLAN [outdated], RELEASE_PROCESS, TASK_DEBUGGING [internal], TASK_PROGRESS_INDICATOR, UI_CAPTURE_PIPELINE); added SEEDING_AND_DEMOS (was linked from README but not in nav); improved nav titles to be keyword-rich.

- **README repositioned — family-first, FHIR demoted to "clinic-ready under the hood".** Reframed the README's hero, "What is", "What's different", and Features sections around household value (bring all your family's health data together, understand your results, track the long view, AI that helps carefully, private by default, for the whole household, make it yours, connect your tools) instead of leading with FHIR/interop architecture. Hero subtitle is now "Self-hosted health records for your household". Added a dedicated **"Clinic-compatible by design"** section lower in the doc that still states the FHIR R4 storage, the 18-resource R4 server facade, the unified catalogs, multi-tenant isolation, RBAC, export/import, and audit provenance — framed as the foundation that lets the same install grow into a clinic-grade record without a rewrite, not as the headline. Scope & Limitations softened to family-self-hosted tone (added "no managed hosted offering", "AI features optional — the rest works without an LLM", "wearable data is one-directional so far"). FHIR no longer appears in the hero, the value props, or any family-oriented feature bullet.

- **README rewrite — accurate, structured, no overclaiming.** Replaced the flat 15-bullet feature list with a grouped, scannable layout: hero with logo, table of contents, "what's different" value props, features organised by domain (clinical data model, workflows, AI, integrations, notifications, security & ops, platform), visual-tour thumbnail grid, a production Docker quick-start (`setup_env.py` → `docker compose … standalone up -d` → `create_system_admin.py`) alongside the dev path, a mermaid architecture diagram, the docs reorganised into the 5 `docs-tree.json` categories, the tech-stack table, and a new honest **Scope & Limitations** section. Toned down marketing language: dropped "Universal", the HIPAA-certification implication, "Full compliance with FHIR" (now "18 R4 resources, advanced conformance is roadmap"), and the generic "Async Processing" bullet (folded into Architecture). Surfaced previously-missing shipped features: the FHIR R4 server facade, Unified Catalog Registry + knowledge graph, Vaccinations/Immunizations, Export/Import backups, the HITL proposal model ("AI never writes clinical data"), the full notifications system, the security posture (Fernet-encrypted keys, prompt-injection guard, HMAC webhooks, audit provenance), the MCP client + webhook + bridge integrations, and PWA/offline/i18n. Added explicit "no medical certification, not HIPAA/GDPR-certified" and the telemetry-outside-FHIR tradeoff to Scope. All 23 doc links + 5 images + logo verified to resolve. Support block moved below features.

- **Popup/dropdown clipping fix on create forms (allergy / examination / medication / clinical events).** Calendar (DatePicker), AI assistant (AIAssistButton), and the selector family (SearchableDropdown, DoctorSelector, OrganizationSelector, CategorySelector, CategoryDropdown, UnitSelector, AnatomyTypeahead) previously rendered their dropdowns inline with `absolute z-50`. Inside modal forms with `overflow-hidden` + `max-h-[90vh]` + `overflow-y-auto`, those dropdowns were clipped at the form/modal boundary — invisible near the bottom edge or on small screens. **New reusable `Popover` primitive** (`components/ui/Popover.tsx`) renders via `createPortal(…, document.body)` with `position: fixed` coordinates from `getBoundingClientRect()`, **auto-flips** when there's no room below (renders above the trigger), **auto-shifts** horizontally to stay in the viewport, and **repositions on scroll/resize** (capture-phase scroll listener, so nested scroll containers inside modal forms also trigger it). All 8 popup components converted; outside-click handling now centralised in one place. Type-check clean; production build green.

- **Hybrid catalog search (trigram + FTS + RRF) for the agentic chatbot + REST + global search.** `search_catalogs`, `search_available_biomarkers`, `search_medications`, and `search_concepts` chatbot tools — plus the `/catalogs/search`, `/search`, and `/concepts/search` REST endpoints — now run through one unified hybrid pipeline in `catalog_search_service.py`. For each catalog, a single SQL runs three matchers (trigram `%` over name/slug/code + `websearch_to_tsquery` FTS over description/indications/info/aliases + `ILIKE` substring fallback) and fuses them via **Reciprocal Rank Fusion** (k=60). Cross-catalog hits are then globally RRF-ranked with a per-type floor so a strong biomarker match can't completely hide an allergy hit. The LLM-facing payload is now enriched: every hit carries `matched_on` (e.g. `["name", "alias", "text"]`), a `ts_headline` snippet showing the match context, and the `score`. Alias matching is fuzzy via `::text ILIKE` (so `"FBS"` now finds `"Fasting Glucose"` via its alias — previously only exact JSONB `@>` containment worked). New migration `j1a2b3c4d5e6` adds per-column trigram GIN indexes (`ix_<table>_<col>_trgm`) + FTS tsvector expression GIN indexes (`ix_<table>_fts`) on biomarker/medication/allergy/anatomy/vaccine/concept catalogs. 11 new tests (`test_hybrid_search.py`); the existing `search_*` per-domain functions keep their ORM-returning signatures (internal delegation only). Plan: `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md` Phase 5.

- **Biomarker detail page reworked into a read-only tabbed view.** The detail page is now purely exploratory — all editing (config panel, inline info editor, delete) moved to the Catalog workspace. Six deep-linkable tabs (URL-synced `/:activeTab`, matching `ExaminationDetail`): **Trend** (the longitudinal chart, default landing), **Clinical** (`info`), **History** (observations table), **Insights** (AI), **Relations** (reuses the catalog `CatalogRelationsGraph`), **Technical** (metadata moved out of the sidebar). Tab bodies extracted into modular components under `components/biomarkers/tabs/`; chart-only state lives inside the Trend tab while shared state (date range, aggregation) stays lifted. Tab strip uses compact wrapping labels (no horizontal scroll) + a modular `TabInfoButton` (i) popover explaining each tab. The page-header subtitle no longer shows the system code (it's in the Technical tab).
- **Catalog forms: IoT telemetry toggle, rich-text editors, chip aliases.** (1) `BiomarkerForm` gains the `is_telemetry` IoT telemetry toggle (flipping it on save triggers the FHIR↔TimescaleDB migration via a confirmation modal in `CatalogWorkspace`). (2) Paragraph-style fields across all catalog forms (medication description/indications/contraindications, allergy/vaccine/concept/generic description) now use a compact rich-text editor (`RichTextField`) instead of plain textareas — the editor auto-detects Markdown (from LLMs) and converts to HTML on load; stored content renders formatted in the catalog Info tab via a new `FormattedText` component + `detectTextFormat` utility (HTML/Markdown/plain). `RichTextEditor` gained a `compact` toolbar variant for modal forms. (3) Aliases upgraded from comma-separated input to a reusable `ChipInput` (type + Enter/comma → removable pill, paste-splitting, Backspace-to-delete, dedupe).
- **Catalog: migration progress visible from the preview pane.** A new `BiomarkerMigrationWatcher` component shows the `MigrationProgressIndicator` (progress bar / failure + retry) inside the catalog preview pane for biomarkers, polling only the selected item (3s, with stall detection) so the FHIR↔telemetry migration can be monitored without leaving the catalog.
- **Graph: optional MiniMap.** `ConceptGraphView` + `CatalogRelationsGraph` gained a `showMiniMap` prop (default true); the biomarker Relations tab disables it (small container).
- **Fix: biomarker catalog edit crashed ("property 'category' has no setter").** The biomarker catalog adapter's `_writable()` filter used `hasattr`, which admitted the computed `category` `@property` (derived from `class_concept`) through to `setattr`. Now uses SQLAlchemy column inspection (matching the base adapter's fix for the identical `is_custom` crash) so `@property`/relationship/annotated fields are excluded from mass-assignment.

- **Taxonomy ↔ Catalogs merge:** concept CRUD folded into the unified Catalogs workspace; `TaxonomyManager.tsx` (1129 LOC) deleted; routes redirect to `/catalogs?type=concept`. `ConceptCatalogAdapter` is read-only (405 on writes); all concept writes flow through `ConceptService` (audit + restore + scope invariant). New `ConceptForm` + `KindChips` + `writeTarget.ts` dispatcher in the frontend. Whole-ontology graph view (`CatalogOntologyGraph`) with List|Graph toggle for all catalog types.
- **Anatomy relations unified into `concept_edges`:** the legacy `anatomy_relations` table is dropped; all ~62 anatomy hierarchy edges (PART_OF, SUPPLIED_BY, BRANCH_OF, etc.) now live in `concept_edges` as `src_type=anatomy, dst_type=anatomy`. The `AnatomyRelation` model + `AnatomyRelationType` enum are deprecated. 6 relation types added to `ConceptRelationType` (now 25 values).
- **Cross-catalog ontology graph:** new `GET /catalogs/graph` endpoint + `whole_catalog_graph()` function returns the full polymorphic graph (concepts, biomarkers, medications, anatomy, allergies, vaccines). Catalog-type filter chips + concept-kind sub-chips + depth BFS + PNG export + "include isolated" toggle.
- **Scope invariant fix:** `ConceptService.create_concept` now derives `scope` from `tenant_id` (was relying on the model default, producing inconsistent `tenant_id`/`scope` pairs).
- **Audit logging:** `ConceptService` now appends `CatalogAuditLog` rows for create/update/delete/restore when an `actor` is provided (REST + AI tools covered; seeds bypass).

### Added
- **Relation-type reference metadata + endpoint.** Each `ConceptRelationType` now carries a human-facing label, an icon, a grouping, and a one-line "when to use this" description, as a single source of truth in a new `app/catalogs/relation_types.py` registry (the "seed" for relation semantics). Exposed via `GET /catalogs/relation-types` → `{"items": [{value, label, group, description, icon}]}`. The registry fails fast at import if it drifts from the enum. The frontend caches it once per session (`loadRelationTypes`/`getRelationType` in `catalogService`) and the `RelationTypeSelect` dropdown renders each option with its icon (`DynamicIcon`, lucide SVG — same convention as catalog-type metadata) and a description, plus an info affordance. New backend test; catalog test suite green.

- **Reusable `CatalogItemPicker` — search-and-select for any catalog item(s).** A new modular, controlled component (`components/catalog/CatalogItemPicker.tsx`) for picking catalog items, usable anywhere a form needs one or many clinical references. Two discovery paths feed one selection: (1) **inline type-ahead** — a debounced cross-catalog search (`searchCatalogs`) with a Portaled results popover showing each hit as `<TYPE-chip> <label>`; (2) a **Browse button** inside the input that opens `CatalogPickerBrowseModal` — the full catalog browser in a popup with a searchable catalog-type dropdown defaulting to **All** (cross-catalog search) or a specific type (`listCatalogItems` with its own search + scope filter), and an Add/Added toggle per row. Supports `mode: 'single' | 'multi'` (single replaces, multi appends + dedupes by `type:id`), and an optional `relationPicker` that surfaces a per-chip relation-type dropdown so selections can carry a relation bind (e.g. `<AFFECTS, biomarker>`). Selected items render as removable chips below the input. The popup reuses the existing `CatalogBrowser` (gains backward-compatible `pickedIds`/`onTogglePick` props for the Add/Added affordance + multi-highlight) and `CatalogTypeSelect` (gains an optional `allowAll` for the cross-catalog entry). Relation options now live in one shared `catalogRelationTypes.ts` (mirror of the backend `ConceptRelationType` enum), replacing the hardcoded copy that was inlined in the editor.

### Changed
- **`CatalogRelationsEditor` refactored onto `CatalogItemPicker`.** The inline cross-catalog search, the Portaled results popover, the relation-type `<select>`, the chip list, and the duplicated `RELATION_OPTIONS` are all removed — the editor is now a thin consumer that maps persisted `concept_edges` ↔ picker selections and reconciles via `createEdge`/`deleteEdge` on change (immediate persistence, same UX as before). ~110 lines of duplicated search/popover plumbing collapse into a `<CatalogItemPicker mode="multi" relationPicker>` call. New `catalogs.picker_*` + `common.remove`/`common.searching` i18n keys (en + el). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean.

### Fixed
- **Catalog item edits not persisted + preview not refreshing.** Editing a catalog item (e.g. a medication) silently failed: the PUT returned a 500 (`property 'is_custom' of 'MedicationCatalog' object has no setter`) because the adapter's `_writable()` filter used `hasattr`, which admitted the computed `is_custom` `@property` (derived from `tenant_id`) — and relationships — through to `setattr`. `_writable` now restricts to real SQLAlchemy mapper columns (`inspect(model).columns`), so computed properties/relationships are excluded from mass-assignment across every catalog. On the frontend the failure was additionally hidden by an **empty `catch { /* toast */ }`** in `handleSave`/`handleDelete` (`CatalogWorkspace`) — the error was swallowed with no toast, so edits looked like they did nothing while relations (which the inline `CatalogRelationsEditor` persists immediately via its own edge calls) appeared to update. Both handlers now surface the backend `detail` via `toast.error`, show a success toast, patch the returned row straight into the local item list (so the Info preview reflects the edit instantly), disable the Save button while in-flight ("Saving…"), and bump a `relationsRevision` counter that drives a new `refreshKey` prop on `CatalogRelationsGraph` so the Relations graph refetches on save (it previously fetched once per item selection and stayed stale until re-selected, without losing the depth/view/node-selection state). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean; 122 catalog tests green.

- **Catalog type dropdown chevron + relations graph fill.** (1) The catalog-type select's chevron sat immediately after the type name instead of at the right edge — the trigger's label span is now `flex-1` so the arrow is pushed to the far right of the button (standard dropdown affordance). (2) The Relations tab graph was locked to a fixed `h-[500px]` and didn't fill the preview pane — `CatalogRelationsGraph` now uses a `flex flex-col h-full` root with the graph canvas as `flex-1 min-h-[400px]` (and the cards view in a `flex-1` scroll area), so it expands to fill all available width and height of the preview pane instead of leaving dead space.

- **Catalog selection contrast + preview header.** (1) The active-row left accent only appeared on the first row because the `border-l-4`/`border-transparent` approach collided with the list's `divide-y` borders — switched the accent to a `box-shadow inset` so it renders on every selected row, and softened the selection fill (`bg-blue-100`→`bg-blue-50`, dark `/50`→`/30`; card `ring-2`→`ring-1 ring-inset`). (2) The preview-pane title was being squeezed out by four labeled action buttons (Edit/History/Delete/Open) — they're now compact icon-only buttons (hover-highlighted, tooltip on hover) so the item title keeps the full remaining width.

### Changed
- **Catalog list: stronger selected-item contrast.** The clicked/active catalog row was nearly invisible (`bg-blue-50/50`). List rows now get a solid `bg-blue-100` / `dark:bg-blue-900/50` plus a blue left-accent bar (`border-l-4 border-blue-500`, transparent when inactive so there's no layout shift); card view gets `bg-blue-50` / `dark:bg-blue-900/40` with a `ring-2 ring-blue-400` and blue border. Selection is now immediately obvious in both light and dark mode.

- **Catalog list: incremental pagination + keyboard navigation.** Two more list upgrades. (1) **Load-more pagination** — the workspace no longer hard-caps browse at 200 items; it now fetches 50 at a time (`limit`/`offset` against the existing `/catalogs/{type}` endpoint) and appends on a **Load more** button at the bottom of the scroll area (spinner state while fetching). This also unblocks the in-memory page-search introduced earlier — clicking Load more expands the searchable set beyond the first page (previously items beyond 200 were invisible + unsearchable). The `mine` scope stays a single all-at-once fetch since its ownership filter is client-side (offset pagination would be wrong on the user-scope set). Count header now reads `N of M` while loading pages, `M total` once complete. (2) **Keyboard navigation** — the list pane is focusable (click it, or it gets a subtle focus ring); **↑/↓** move the selection through the (filtered + sorted) rows and drive the preview pane, **Esc** clears the selection, and the selected row auto-scrolls into view (`scrollIntoView({block:'nearest'})`, which doesn't disturb click selection). A hover tooltip hints the shortcuts. New `catalogs.load_more` / `loading_more` / `keyboard_hint` i18n keys (en + el). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean.

- **Catalog search moved to the global page-search; search-match highlighting + loading skeletons.** The catalog workspace no longer has its own search box — item search is now the shared header **SearchLauncher** in *Current Page* mode. `CatalogWorkspace` opts into page-search (`setIsPageSearchSupported(true)` on mount) and filters the loaded items **in-memory** against `pageSearchTerm` (the backend `?search=` param is no longer sent on browse); the local `search` state + the `<input>` in `CatalogToolbar` are removed. Two complementary list polish items ship with it: (1) **search-match highlighting** — a `Highlight` helper wraps case-insensitive matches of the active term in `<mark>` on each row's title and description (list + card views), so it's obvious *why* a row matched; `CatalogBrowser` gains a `searchTerm` prop. (2) **Loading skeletons** — the full-section spinner is replaced by animated skeleton rows (list) / cards (card view) that match the real layout, reducing perceived load time and layout shift. The header's active-search chip continues to show/clear the active term. `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean.

- **Catalog list: clickable tags, client-side sort header, and differentiated empty states.** Three upgrades to the catalog item list (`CatalogBrowser`). (1) **Clickable tags** — the scope badge and the taxonomy class badge on each row are now interactive: clicking a scope badge (System / Tenant / Yours) toggles the workspace scope filter to that tier (and marks itself active with a ring), and clicking a class badge toggles that class in the `?class=` filter (works for any catalog that carries a `class_concept_*`, not just anatomy); the `ScopeBadge` gained optional `onClick`/`active` props (it renders as a `<button>` when clickable, plain `<span>` otherwise, so the preview-pane badges stay non-interactive). (2) **Sort header** — a sticky bar above the scroll area offers client-side sort by **Name / Updated / Relations** (asc/desc toggle via the arrow icon; Updated/Relations default to desc) plus a live count that reads `N total` normally and `N of M` when a filter narrows the visible set (replaces the old count line buried at the bottom). (3) **Empty states** — instead of a flat "No items found." the list now distinguishes *no matches* (search/filter active → icon + hint + a **Clear filters** button that resets search/scope/class) from *no items yet* (fresh catalog → hint pointing at New). Also dropped the now-redundant per-row **View relations** button (the Relations tab in the preview already covers it; `onViewRelations` prop + the `viewRelations` handler removed). New `catalogs.sort_*` / `catalogs.count_of` / `catalogs.no_matches*` / `catalogs.empty_*` + `common.clear_filters` i18n keys (en + el). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean.

- **Catalog list rows decluttered; edit/history/delete moved to the preview pane only.** Each list row was carrying five action buttons (Open / Edit / Relations / History / Delete) alongside inline tags, which crowded the title and overlapped it when names were long. The list now shows only the lightweight **View relations** + **Open in domain** inline actions; **Edit / History / Delete** live exclusively in the preview pane (a **Delete** button was added to the desktop preview header, and Edit/History/Delete icon buttons to the mobile full-screen popup, so mobile users keep access). Row layout reworked: the title gets its own full-width line (no longer shares a flex row with the scope/class badges → no truncation overlap), the description switched from a harsh 80-char slice to `line-clamp-2` (proper two-line wrap), and the scope + class badges moved to a dedicated right-aligned column. Row padding bumped (`py-3`→`py-3.5`) for a slightly taller, more legible item. `CatalogBrowser` is fully presentational now (its `onEdit`/`onDelete`/`onHistory` props are dropped — the workspace owns those actions). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean.

- **Catalogs workspace reworked into a layered shell (Phase 3 of the catalogs UI rework).** The per-type workspace is now a master-detail-with-tabs instead of a Browser/Relations tab toggle: **Layer 1** is an always-visible item browser + an item-selector dropdown (default "All items") that sets `?item=`; **Layer 2** is a tab bar — **Info | Relations | <custom>**. The Relations tab is no longer disabled when nothing is selected: with "All" it renders a new **relation-centric index** (`CatalogRelationsIndex`) — every item with outgoing edges grouped by relation type (TREATS / AFFECTS / …), each clickable to select that item — reusing the single `?include=relations` fetch (no extra round-trip); with an item selected it shows that item's cross-catalog graph. The click-to-preview **drawer is removed** (`CatalogItemDrawer` deleted); item detail now renders inline in the **Info** tab (`CatalogItemInfo`). `CatalogBrowser` is now presentational (the workspace owns item-loading + the edit/audit modals, so the New button and the Info tab's Edit button share one modal). Selecting an item no longer forces a tab switch — it drives both Info and Relations. The **Ranges** (biomarker), **Interactions** (medication) and **Atlas** (anatomy) custom tabs are removed (the Info/Relations tabs + dedicated domain pages cover them); the custom-tab registry is retained for future tabs. New `catalogs.*` i18n keys (en + el). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean (0 errors). See `dev/plans/catalogs-ui-rework-2026-07-09.md`.

### Added
- **Anatomy class chips + badges in the catalog (Phase 4 of the catalogs UI rework).** `/catalogs?type=anatomy` now shows each item's anatomy class as a colored badge (Organ / Region / System / Joint / …, read from the Phase-2 `class_concept_slug`/`class_concept_name` projection) and offers **multi-select class filter chips** in Layer 1 — the chips fetch the `anatomy_class` concepts (`GET /catalogs/concept?kind=anatomy_class`) and filter the list via `?class=organ,region,…`. The class badge is generic (renders on any catalog item that carries a `class_concept_name`, incl. biomarkers). `listCatalogItems` + the `CatalogItem` type gain `kind` / `class` / `class_concept_*`. The Anatomy Explorer's broken category filter is also unblocked: the landing "systems" fetch now uses `?class=system` (the legacy `?category=` was silently ignored by the backend) and system dots/labels read `class_concept_slug`/`class_concept_name`. `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean. See `dev/plans/catalogs-ui-rework-2026-07-09.md`.

- **Catalog class filter + projection (Phase 2 of the catalogs UI rework).** The taxonomy-class concept is now visible and filterable across catalogs, via one registry-driven mechanism. `GET /catalogs/{type}` gains `?class=<slug>` (comma-list OK) — the adapter resolves the slug → concept id and filters on the descriptor's `concept_link` FK column, so it works for *every* catalog that carries a `class_concept_id` (anatomy, biomarker, medication, allergy, vaccine) with no per-catalog code. Anatomy + biomarker items now serialize `class_concept_slug` + `class_concept_name` (read off the selectin-loaded `class_concept` relation) — so e.g. Thyroid shows as "Organ" instead of a bare UUID, and ALT shows its biomarker class. `GET /catalogs/concept?kind=<ConceptKind>` filters concepts by `primary_kind`. The dedicated `/anatomy` endpoint mirrors this: `?class=<slug>` + class projection on list/detail, and `POST/PATCH /anatomy` accept `class_concept_slug` (resolved to `class_concept_id`) so callers needn't know the UUID. 9 new tests (`test_catalog_concept_link.py`, `test_anatomy_class_projection.py`); 293 related tests green. See `dev/plans/catalogs-ui-rework-2026-07-09.md`.

### Removed
- **Legacy `AnatomyCategory` enum dropped (Phase 2, clean rebuild).** The uppercase `AnatomyCategory` enum (SYSTEM/REGION/ORGAN/…) — a vestige of the pre-concept `category` column — is deleted entirely. `data/seeds/anatomy_structures.json` is migrated to the lossless `class_concept_slug` form (e.g. `"category": "ORGAN"` → `"class_concept_slug": "organ"`); the `_ANATOMY_CATEGORY_TO_CONCEPT_SLUG` map + legacy fallback branch in `seed_service` and the inverse map in `seed_export_service` are removed (the `class_concept_slug` path is now the only path). The obsolete `test_anatomy_seed_falls_back_to_legacy_category` test is deleted. (Frontend `AnatomyCategory` type + Anatomy Explorer category chips are rewritten to class slugs in Phase 4.)

### Fixed
- **Seed ordering: `concepts` now seeds before `body_parts` (and `default_catalog`).** `SeedService._SEED_STAGE_NAMES` ran `body_parts` (anatomy) before `concepts`, so on a fresh DB the `class_concept_slug` → `class_concept_id` resolution found no `anatomy_class` concepts and **every anatomy row got `class_concept_id = NULL`** (0/54 resolved). The catalog class chips/filter/projection (Phase 2–4) therefore showed nothing until a re-seed over an already-populated DB. `concepts` is now first in the order (it's dependency-free; `body_parts`, `default_catalog`, `concept_edges`, and `biomarker_panels` all resolve concept slugs). New regression test `test_seed_order.py` asserts every seeded anatomy structure resolves its class (thyroid → `organ`/`Organ`).

- **Catalogs layering + sidebar nav (Phase 1 of the catalogs UI rework).** Two layering bugs and a nav mismatch are fixed via a principled stacking-context approach rather than renumbering z-indexes. (1) The item-detail drawer (`CatalogItemDrawer`) and the edit modal previously rendered *under* the sidebar's hover popups (`z-100`) and collapse handle (`z-960`); the Sidebar root now carries `isolate` (`isolation: isolate`), which scopes all of its internal z-indexes into their own stacking context so they can never overlay a body-level Portal again. (2) A documented Tailwind `zIndex` scale (`dropdown: 100`, `modal: 1000`, `drawer: 1100`, `toast: 1200`) replaces the pile of magic numbers; the drawer uses `z-drawer`, the edit modal + shared `<Modal>` use `z-modal`. (3) The edit modal is restructured into `flex flex-col max-h-[90vh]` (fixed header/footer, scrollable middle) and the inline relations-editor's target-search popover is now rendered via `<Portal>` at `z-dropdown` anchored to the input (`getBoundingClientRect`, repositioned on scroll/resize) — so it escapes the modal's scroll container and is no longer clipped (no more scrolling the form to see the full dropdown). (4) Sidebar "Catalogs" group: the **Anatomy** sub-item now points at `/catalogs?type=anatomy` (was `/anatomy`, which left the workspace) and a new **Concepts** → `/catalogs?type=concept` entry is added; new `common.concepts` / `common.anatomy` i18n keys (en + el). The `/anatomy` explorer route is unchanged (reachable via the catalog's "Open in domain view"). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean (0 errors). See `dev/plans/catalogs-ui-rework-2026-07-09.md`.
- **Backend test pythonpath (pre-existing).** `pytest.ini` `pythonpath` now includes the repo root (`.` + `..`) so the `integrations` package (moved out of `backend/` to the repo root in commit 115f687) resolves — the test suite could not even load `conftest.py` before this.

### Added
- **Catalog item UX rework — type-specific forms, preview drawer, relations editor, item switcher, relation counts.** Replaces the thin generic editor with a richer, type-aware interaction model:
  - **Per-type forms** (registry at `components/catalog/forms/`): biomarker (slug/code/aliases/ref-range/unit), medication (indications/dosage/side-effects/contraindications), allergy (category enum/reactions), vaccine (CVX/target-diseases), generic fallback. Field lists mirror the backend create schemas.
  - **Inline relations editor** in the edit modal (`CatalogRelationsEditor`): manage the item's outgoing `concept_edges` — add a relation by picking a relation type + searching ANY catalog for the target (cross-catalog), remove existing edges as chips. Uses the polymorphic `POST/DELETE /concept-edges` endpoints.
  - **Click-to-preview drawer** (`CatalogItemDrawer`): clicking a row now opens a right-side slide-over showing the full item detail + scope badge + audit timestamp, with Edit / Relations / History / Open-in-domain as explicit actions (no longer drops straight into edit).
  - **Searchable item switcher** in the Relations tab (`CatalogItemSwitcher`): a combobox showing the current item, search-scoped to the active type, to swap `?item=` without leaving the tab.
  - **Relation counts in the list**: `GET /catalogs/{type}` gains `?include=relations` (new `count_relations` batch query — N+1-safe) annotating each item with `relation_count` + `relation_breakdown`; both list rows and cards show a `≁ N` chip. 3 new backend tests (`test_catalog_relation_counts.py`). `npm run build` + `npm run lint` clean.

- **Catalog relations — graph + cards view (Phase E).** The Relations tab now actually renders and offers two synchronized views. **Root-cause fix:** `ConceptGraphView`'s wrapper applied a hardcoded `h-full` *alongside* the caller's `h-[500px]` — two conflicting `height` declarations, so when `h-full` won (parent had no height) the graph was 0px tall and React Flow errored ("parent container needs a width and a height"). `h-full` is now the *overridable default* `className`, and `CatalogRelationsGraph` wraps the graph in an explicit `h-[500px]` container (mirroring the working TaxonomyManager pattern). New **Graph ⇄ Cards sub-tab toggle** within the Relations tab: the cards view (`CatalogRelationsCards`) lists the item's `concept_edges` grouped by relation type (TREATS / PREVENTS / AFFECTS / …), each card clickable → navigates to the connected item in the catalog. Clear **empty-state** prompt ("Select an item from the Browser tab…") when the Relations tab is opened with no item selected. `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean. See `dev/plans/catalog-access-control-and-ui-2026-07-08.md`.

- **Catalog unified UI — Phase D (list/card views + per-type custom tabs + left-rail scope filter).** Every catalog type now renders through one consistent, configurable UI shell. The Browser tab gains a **list/card view toggle** (compact rows vs. richer cards with scope badge + description + "Updated Xh ago" + actions, per plan §3.2). A new **per-type custom-tab registry** (`components/catalog/tabs/catalogTabs.tsx`) makes adding a tab = one component + one entry; three functional starters ship: **Biomarker → "Ranges"** (inline-editable reference-range table: min/max/unit per biomarker, scope-aware), **Anatomy → "Atlas"** (responsive card-grid index of body parts with standard codes + scope badges, linking to the Anatomy Explorer), and **Medication → "Interactions"** (expand-a-medication browser surfacing its `TREATS` / `CONTRAINDICATES` / `INDICATES` / `CAUSED_BY` edges from the polymorphic graph, grouped by relation type). Custom tabs render alongside the built-in Browser + Relations tabs in `CatalogWorkspace`. The **scope filter moved to the left rail** (All / System / Tenant / **Mine**) as a workspace-level control; "Mine" narrows to the current user's user-scope items (fetches `?scope=user` then filters by `created_by`); `CatalogBrowser` now accepts controlled `scopeFilter` / `onScopeFilterChange` props (hiding its in-toolbar `<select>` when the workspace drives it). New `catalogs.*` i18n keys (en + el): tab labels, view-toggle titles, column headers, help text. `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean. See `dev/plans/catalog-access-control-and-ui-2026-07-08.md`.

- **Catalog routing consolidation — Phase C.** All catalog browsing now lives at one unified `/catalogs?type={type}` route (all authenticated users), replacing the scattered `/{type}/catalog` per-type pages and the SYSTEM_ADMIN-only `/admin/catalogs` workspace. The unified `CatalogWorkspace` moved from `pages/Admin/Catalogs/` to `pages/Catalogs/` (no longer admin-prefixed) and dropped its "Administration" breadcrumb. The four legacy routes (`/biomarkers/catalog`, `/medications/catalog`, `/vaccines/catalog`, `/allergies/catalog`) now `<Navigate>` to `/catalogs?type=…` (no transition period), and `/admin/catalogs` redirects to `/catalogs` for stale bookmarks. The dedicated `BiomarkerCatalog`, `MedicationCatalog`, and generic `CatalogPage` components are **removed** (clean rebuild — their rich forms become custom tabs in Phase D; common name/description editing already works via `CatalogBrowser`). The sidebar "Catalogs" group sub-items now point at `/catalogs?type=…`, and `isSubActive` became query-string-aware so the right catalog type highlights. Every internal link retargeted: SearchLauncher (also fixes a latent bug where `/admin/catalogs?vaccine` used a bare flag instead of `?type=vaccine`), the biomarker + medication detail "Manage in Catalogs" buttons, the biomarker trends / medication list "open catalog" buttons, and the post-delete redirects. The settings nav's redundant `/admin/catalogs` entry is removed (the workspace is now top-level nav). The "concept" type's "Open Taxonomy Manager" link is now role-aware (`/admin/system/taxonomy` for SYSTEM_ADMIN, `/examinations/categories` for everyone else, since TaxonomyManager mounts at both). The legacy import page (`/admin/system/catalogs` → `CatalogManagement`) stays SYSTEM_ADMIN-only. `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean. See `dev/plans/catalog-access-control-and-ui-2026-07-08.md`.

- **Catalog audit log — Phase B (backend).** Every catalog CRUD operation now appends an immutable `CatalogAuditLog` row (who / what / operation / scope-change / item snapshot), giving a durable record of who changed what, when, and (for promote/demote) the scope transition. New `CatalogAuditLog` model (`app/models/catalog_audit_model.py`) + migration `f7a8b9c0d1e2` — append-only, with `user_email` and `item_name` denormalized so the trail survives user/item deletion; `tenant_id`/`user_id` are deliberately FK-less for the same reason (added to the tenant-FK test's documented exception set). New `app/services/catalog_audit_service.py` (`record` / `record_from_obj` / `list_history`) — recording is best-effort at two levels (the service swallows commit errors, and the adapter's `_audit` wraps the call) so an audit failure never aborts the parent catalog write. Wired into `BaseCatalogAdapter` + `BiomarkerCatalogAdapter`: create/update/delete/promote each append a row after commit (delete captures the item snapshot before the row is gone; promote records `from_scope`→`to_scope`). Each adapter gains a `catalog_type` attribute (stamped by `registrations.py`) so rows record the catalog type. `BiomarkerCatalogAdapter` now inherits from `BaseCatalogAdapter` (gaining the audit helpers + `catalog_type`) while keeping its Unit-join overrides. New endpoint `GET /catalogs/{type}/{id}/history` returns the trail newest-first, tenant-scoped (the item must be visible to the caller — 404 otherwise — so the trail never leaks cross-tenant). See `dev/plans/catalog-access-control-and-ui-2026-07-08.md`. 7 new tests in `test_catalog_audit.py` (create/update/delete/promote → audit rows, history endpoint ordering + tenant-scoping, best-effort audit failure).
- **Catalog audit log — Phase B (frontend).** The catalog browser now surfaces the ownership + audit model. Every item row shows a colored **scope badge** (`ScopeBadge` — system=violet, tenant=blue, yours=green, user=amber; the "yours" vs "user" distinction uses the current user id vs `created_by`) and a relative "Updated Xh ago" timestamp (via `date-fns` `formatDistanceToNow`, locale-aware). A scope **filter** dropdown narrows the list (`All` / `System` / `Tenant` / `User`, wired to the `?scope=` query param). A **History** button on each row opens an `AuditHistoryModal` (reusing the shared `<Modal>` shell) showing the item's audit trail newest-first — operation badge, scope transition (`from → to`), the denormalized `user_email`, and a relative timestamp. New `CatalogItem` / `CatalogScope` / `CatalogAuditEntry` types; `getCatalogItemHistory` service wrapper; `listCatalogItems` gains a `scope` param. New `catalogs.*` i18n namespace (en + el). `npm run build` (tsc strict) + `npm run lint` clean. See `dev/plans/catalog-access-control-and-ui-2026-07-08.md`.

- **Catalog ownership-based access control — Phase A (scope tiers).** Catalog access is now ownership-based instead of pure role-based, so any user can contribute without breaking curated data. Every catalog item (biomarker, medication, allergy, vaccine, anatomy, concept) carries an explicit `scope` of `system` | `tenant` | `user` (new `CatalogScope` enum + nullable-default `scope` column via migration `e6f7a8b9c0d1`, backfilled from `tenant_id`: NULL→system, non-NULL→tenant). The rewritten `CatalogAccessPolicy` decides access by `(role, item.scope, ownership)`: **any authenticated user may CREATE** — a SYSTEM_ADMIN create lands in system-scope (canonical, `tenant_id=NULL`), ADMIN/MANAGER in tenant-scope, USER in user-scope (visible to the whole tenant, editable only by the creator + admins). Update/delete of system-scope requires SYSTEM_ADMIN; tenant-scope requires ADMIN/MANAGER; user-scope requires the creator OR an admin. New `POST /catalogs/{type}/{id}/promote` endpoint transitions scope (user↔tenant needs ADMIN/MANAGER; anything involving system needs SYSTEM_ADMIN; promote-to-system clears `tenant_id`, demote-to-tenant sets it). `GET /catalogs/{type}` gains a `?scope=system|tenant|user` filter. The `CatalogServiceProtocol` gains `promote_scope()`; both `BaseCatalogAdapter` and the specialised `BiomarkerCatalogAdapter` are fully scope-aware (create stamps scope+tenant_id+created_by; update/delete consult ownership). The domain endpoints/services (biomarker, medication, allergy, vaccine) are migrated to the same scope+ownership model (a USER can now create via `/biomarkers/`, `/medications/catalog`, etc., landing in user-scope). `anatomy_structures` gained the `AuditMixin` columns (`created_by`/`updated_by`) so the ownership model is uniform across all catalogs. See `dev/plans/catalog-access-control-and-ui-2026-07-08.md`. 55 new tests in `test_catalog_scope_access.py` (create→role-derived scope, ownership matrix, promote/demote gating, scope filter, migration backfill) + updated RBAC/domain tests for the new USER-create semantics.

- **Catalog LLM tools (Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 8).** The agentic chatbot can now answer cross-catalog questions via two new tools registered in the tool registry. `search_catalogs(query, types?, limit?)` — ranked trigram search across every registered catalog (biomarkers, medications, vaccines, allergies, anatomy, diseases) in one call; returns `{type, id, label}` hits; auto-covers newly-registered catalogs. `explore_catalog_relations(type, id, max_depth?, relations?)` — multi-hop graph traversal over the polymorphic `concept_edges` graph; answers "which organ does this biomarker affect?", "what diseases does this vaccine prevent?", "what medications treat this disease?"; the `relations` whitelist prunes to specific edge types (e.g. `["PREVENTS"]`). Both tools are pure read paths over the registry (tenant-scoped, read-only — AI never writes; proposals go through HITL). The agent system prompt gains a CATALOG & KNOWLEDGE-GRAPH RULES section directing the LLM to prefer `search_catalogs` for cross-domain discovery and `explore_catalog_relations` for relational questions. A type alias (`vaccine` → `immunization`) keeps the LLM-facing vocabulary consistent with search results. See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 9 new tests (search finds medication/disease, types filter, short-query empty, relations from medication + vaccine, relation whitelist, registration + get_tools inclusion).
- **Unified Catalogs admin workspace (Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 7).** One admin screen manages every clinical reference catalog. New `/admin/catalogs` page (`CatalogWorkspace`) renders a **registry-driven** left rail from `GET /catalogs` (UI meta from the backend `CatalogRegistry`) — so newly-registered catalogs appear automatically with no hardcoded nav. Each type offers two tabs: **Browser** (`<CatalogBrowser>` — searchable list + create/edit/delete via the `/catalogs/{type}` CRUD routes + "Open in domain view" deep links to existing detail pages) and **Relations** (`<CatalogRelationsGraph>` — the cross-catalog `concept_edges` graph, reusing the existing `ConceptGraphView` with an adapter that maps the `/catalogs/{type}/{id}/relations` response into the graph node/edge shapes; this is the visual "which organ does this biomarker affect? what treats this disease?"). The "concept" type links out to the existing `TaxonomyManager`. New `services/catalogService.ts` (typed wrapper for all `/catalogs` endpoints) + `types/catalog.ts`. The global search box (`SearchLauncher`) now navigates catalog-type results (anatomy, allergy, vaccine, concept) and renders type-appropriate icons — the mock-results fallback is removed (the backend `/search` already aggregates `/catalogs/search`). "Manage in Catalogs" links added to the biomarker + medication detail pages' toolbars. The settings nav replaces the separate "Clinical Ontology" + "Taxonomy" entries with one "Catalogs" entry → `/admin/catalogs`. Backend fix: the anatomy catalog's `ui.icon` corrected from the nonexistent `"Body"` to `"PersonStanding"` (a valid lucide-react export). `npm run build` (tsc strict + vite) + `npm run lint` clean. See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`.
- **Diseases as concepts + FHIR CodeSystem/ValueSet (Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 6).** Illness/disease reference data now exists as first-class `kind=disease` concepts and is FHIR-queryable. New `data/seeds/diseases.json` seeds 57 curated ICD-10 disease concepts (top causes of morbidity/mortality + all vaccine-target diseases: measles, mumps, rubella, influenza, COVID-19, tetanus, diphtheria, pertussis, hepatitis B, HPV, cervical cancer, pneumococcal pneumonia) via a new `seed_diseases` stage in the ordered `seed_all` pipeline — diseases live as concepts so they inherit full CRUD/search/edges/FHIR for free via the concept layer (no new table). The cross-domain `concept_edges` graph is extended with the deferred Phase 3/5 edges: specialty `EXAMINES` disease (cardiology→CAD, endocrinology→diabetes, pulmonology→asthma, …), medication `TREATS` disease (metformin→T2DM, lisinopril→hypertension, atorvastatin→hypercholesterolemia, …), medication `CONTRAINDICATES` disease (aspirin→peptic-ulcer, metformin→CKD), and vaccine `PREVENTS` disease (MMR→measles/mumps/rubella, HPV→HPV+cervical-cancer, …) — the seed loader gained a `"vaccine"` endpoint branch (resolves `VaccineCatalog` by slug) so `GET /catalogs/{type}/{id}/relations` now answers "what does the MMR vaccine prevent?" and "what treats type-2-diabetes?" end-to-end. The FHIR R4 facade publishes the disease vocabulary as two new computed terminology resources: `GET /fhir/R4/CodeSystem/ha-diseases` (a `CodeSystem` with `content=complete` + every disease's ICD-10 code/display) and `GET /fhir/R4/ValueSet/ha-diseases` (a `ValueSet` composing the ICD-10 system) — both validate against `fhir.resources`. These are the first **computed** facade resources (no backing table): `ResourceEntry` gained optional `read_fn`/`search_fn` hooks that bypass the generic table-query dispatcher and project from the `concepts` table; the CapabilityStatement advertises both. `SeedExportService` gained `export_diseases` (+ `diseases.json` in `EXPORTERS`) as the strict inverse of `seed_diseases`, and `export_concepts` now excludes disease-kind concepts so re-exporting an unchanged DB remains a git no-op; the edge export's slug maps now cover `MEDICATION` (by name) + `IMMUNIZATION` (by slug) endpoints. See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 24 new tests (5 disease-seed idempotency/code-coverage, 8 cross-domain edge resolution incl. graph traverse, 10 CodeSystem/ValueSet facade incl. CapabilityStatement + 405-on-write, 1 diseases-export round-trip). **Out of scope:** Anatomy `BodyStructure` FHIR resource (deferred per decision §16.2); frontend disease management folds into the existing TaxonomyManager (Phase 7).
- **Vaccines & immunizations (Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 5).** Vaccinations are implemented end-to-end, mirroring the medications pattern. New tables `vaccine_catalog` (CVX-coded reference definitions, with `class_concept_id` taxonomy hook) + `patient_immunizations` (dose-administered patient-instance records) via migration `d5e6f7a8b9c0`. REST CRUD at `/vaccines/catalog*` (RBAC: USER read-only, ADMIN/MANAGER tenant, SYSTEM_ADMIN global) + `/vaccines/patient/{id}` + per-record `/vaccines/{id}` (patient-access scoped via `check_immunization_access`). FHIR R4: `PatientImmunization.to_fhir_dict()` → canonical `Immunization` (status, vaccineCode, patient, occurrenceDateTime, lotNumber, protocolApplied.doseNumberPositiveInt); `VaccineCatalog.to_fhir_dict()` → `Medication`. Registered `Immunization` as a 16th facade resource (read + search-type) with a `param_filter` mapping `date`→`administered_at` + `vaccine-code`→JSONB text. Both write paths pass the `assert_valid_fhir` gate. Vaccines are registered in the `CatalogRegistry` (`VaccineCatalogAdapter`) + the `IMMUNIZATION` endpoint resolver, so they appear in `/catalogs/vaccine`, `/catalogs/search`, and the cross-catalog graph automatically. Seeded 7 CVX-coded vaccines (MMR, influenza, COVID-19 mRNA, Tdap, HepB, HPV, PCV) via a new `seed_vaccines` stage. See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 11 new tests (catalog CRUD+RBAC, patient-instance CRUD+access, FHIR projections, facade search, registry integration, migration). **Deferred:** `PREVENTS` vaccine→disease edges (need disease concepts → Phase 6); dedicated frontend pages (Phase 7 — vaccines already surface in `/catalogs`).
- **Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 4: registry-driven cross-catalog search.** One dispatcher searches every registered catalog at once. `search_catalogs(db, tenant_id, q, types=, limit=)` (in `catalog_search_service.py`) iterates the `CatalogRegistry` and calls each adapter's new `search()` method — typo-tolerant `pg_trgm` trigram matching over the descriptor's `search_columns` with an `ilike` fallback, ranked by `similarity(label_column, q)`, returning uniform `{type, id, label}` hits. Exposed at `GET /catalogs/search?q=&types=&limit=` (anatomy, concepts, and allergies now surface, not just medications + biomarkers). The global `GET /search` catalog portion is rewired to delegate to the dispatcher, so newly-registered catalogs appear in global search automatically — the hardcoded per-entity blocks are gone. Adding a catalog to search = registering it (the descriptor already declares `search_columns`). See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 9 new tests (dispatcher all-types/type-filter/short-query/tenant-scope/unknown-type, `/catalogs/search` endpoint, `/search` now includes anatomy+concept+allergy).
- **Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 3: cross-domain seed edges + single link system.** The polymorphic `concept_edges` graph is now the **only** cross-domain link system. Migration `c4d5e6f7a8b9` drops the two legacy biomarker link tables: `biomarker_relationships` (was dead code) and `biomarker_event_correlations` (its live readers — `clinical_event_service` recommended-biomarker insight + the `POST/GET/DELETE /clinical-events/types/{id}/biomarkers` CRUD — were rewritten first to query `concept_edges`, where biomarker↔clinical_event_type is a `MONITORS` edge with `correlation_type`/`description` on the edge's `properties` JSONB). The ORM classes, schema classes, and the legacy `scripts/seed_biomarkers.py` correlation writes are removed. `concept_edges.json` is extended with cross-domain biomarker→anatomy `AFFECTS` edges (creatinine→kidneys, tsh→thyroid, glucose→pancreas, lipids→cardiovascular-system) + biomarker→body-system `INDICATES` edges — these power the headline "which organ does this biomarker affect?" query via `GET /catalogs/{type}/{id}/relations`. The seed loader gained a `"medication"` endpoint branch (resolves `MedicationCatalog` by name), enabling medication→disease edges when Phase 6 seeds disease concepts. See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 6 new tests (correlation CRUD via edges, seed loader, table-drop verification, model-registry cleanup). **Note:** medication→disease / specialty→disease edges are deferred to Phase 6 (require disease concepts).
- **Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 2: cross-catalog graph completion.** The polymorphic `concept_edges` link system is now finished and queryable end-to-end. New `app/services/catalog_graph_service.traverse()` does a depth-bounded (1–5), cycle-safe, tenant-scoped **recursive-CTE** traversal from any `(type, id)` start node, returning a display-ready `{start, nodes, edges}` payload (endpoints resolved via the resolver registry). Exposed at `GET /catalogs/{type}/{id}/relations?depth=&relation=&include_proposed=` — this is the headline query: "which organ does this biomarker affect? what treats that disease?" The endpoint-resolver registry now covers **7 of 11** `EdgeEndpointType` values (added medication, allergy, clinical_event_type). Migration `a1b2c3d4e5f7` adds `class_concept_id` (nullable FK→concepts.id, indexed) to `medication_catalog` and `allergy_catalog`, giving every catalog a native taxonomy classification on the established `<role>_concept_id` convention; adds the `AFFECTS` value to the `conceptrelationtype` PG enum (the biomarker→anatomy semantic link). **Decision refined:** the legacy `AllergyCategory` enum is **kept** (it backs the FHIR `AllergyIntolerance.category` closed value set on both the catalog and patient-instance models); `class_concept_id` is added alongside it. See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 13 new tests (resolver extension, traverse depth/cycle/whitelist/proposed-filter, relations endpoint, migration column presence, AFFECTS round-trip).
- **Unified Catalog Registry — Phase 1: RBAC normalization + CRUD completion.** The uniform `CatalogAccessPolicy` (USER = read-only; ADMIN/MANAGER = tenant-scoped writes; SYSTEM_ADMIN = global writes + bypass) is now enforced across **all** catalog write surfaces — closing the pre-Phase-1 gaps where a `USER` could `DELETE /biomarkers/{id}` and biomarker reads leaked across tenants. Enforced both on the `/catalogs` meta-layer write routes (`POST/PUT/DELETE /catalogs/{type}[/{id}]`, now wired through the adapter `create/update/delete`) and on the domain endpoints (biomarker/medication/allergy catalog create/update/delete). `CatalogPermissionDenied` is mapped to HTTP 403 by a new global handler in `main.py`. Allergy catalog CRUD is **completed** (get-one `GET /allergies/catalog/{id}`, update `PUT`, delete `DELETE` were missing — now full round-trip + `AllergyCatalogUpdate` schema). Medication catalog **delete** added (`DELETE /medications/catalog/{id}`). Biomarker reads are now tenant-scoped (`or_(tenant_id == caller, tenant_id IS NULL)`) and bulk-delete is restricted to the caller's own tenant rows. Allergy/medication **patient-instance** routes are unchanged. See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 25 new tests (15 RBAC parametrized over biomarker/medication/allergy × the role/scope matrix + 10 domain CRUD incl. the biomarker tenant-scope regression). AllergyCatalog `to_fhir_dict` deferred to the facade phase (the instance gate was already closed in audit C13; the catalog table has no FHIR JSONB).
- **Unified Catalog Registry foundation (Phase 0).** A new `app/catalogs/` package introduces a declarative `CatalogRegistry` + `CatalogDescriptor` contract that all clinical catalogs (anatomy, taxonomy, biomarkers, medications, allergies — vaccines/diseases in later phases) conform to, plus a uniform `CatalogAccessPolicy` RBAC value object and a `CatalogServiceProtocol`. Each catalog registers once (model, service adapter, search columns, concept-link, `EdgeEndpointType`, graph resolver, FHIR projector, UI metadata) and gains unified read access via a new thin `/catalogs` meta-layer: `GET /catalogs` (registered types + UI meta, drives the future admin workspace left rail), `GET /catalogs/{type}` (tenant-scoped list, global+caller's tenant), and `GET /catalogs/{type}/{id}` (get-one). The meta-layer **complements** (does not replace) the domain endpoints — it dispatches by type to the registered adapter. This is the foundation for cross-catalog search (Phase 4), the polymorphic graph (Phase 2), vaccines (Phase 5), diseases-as-concepts (Phase 6), the unified admin workspace (Phase 7), and two LLM tools (Phase 8). Domain endpoints are unchanged; the adapters tenant-scope reads correctly (the biomarker adapter fixes the legacy global-leak that Phase 1 will also fix on the domain endpoint). See `dev/plans/unified-catalog-architecture-2026-07-08.md`. 21 tests (12 registry unit + 9 real-DB API incl. cross-tenant isolation).
- **Bidirectional examination ↔ clinical-event surfacing.** An examination's REST response now includes a `clinical_events` array (id/title/status/reason of the journeys it belongs to, capped at 20), and its FHIR `Encounter` projection emits real `diagnosis[].condition.reference = "Condition/{id}"` entries for each linked `ClinicalEvent`. This closes a documented-but-unimplemented gap (the `to_fhir_dict` comment promised Condition references "when a ClinicalEvent row is linked via EventExaminationLink" — the code never produced them) and makes navigation between visits and journeys work in both directions. The examination list + detail endpoints now eager-load `event_links.event`; `ExaminationResponse` carries the new field. 1 real-DB test (REST surfacing + Encounter Condition reference).
- **`BiomarkerEventCorrelation` CRUD endpoints.** `POST /clinical-events/types/{type_id}/biomarkers` and `DELETE /clinical-events/types/{type_id}/biomarkers/{biomarker_id}` let admins manage which biomarkers are clinically relevant to monitor for a given journey type. Previously correlations were seed-script-only — there was no API or UI to define them. The create is idempotent on the (type, biomarker) pair (re-adding updates `correlation_type`/`description` in place rather than 409-ing). The `ClinicalEventEngine`'s `recommended_biomarkers` insight reads from these correlations end-to-end (create a correlation → it surfaces in `/clinical-events/{id}/insights`). 2 real-DB tests (CRUD lifecycle + recommendation flow-through).
- **Behavior-driving Clinical Event types + a `ClinicalEventEngine`.** `ClinicalEventType` is promoted from a passive form-schema holder into a journey *template* via four new JSONB columns (migration `f2c3d4e5f6a7`): `severity_scale`, `phases` (e.g. trimesters), `milestones` (with `alert_before_days`), and `default_duration_days`.
